Pinyin: Chāoshì zhǐ jiēshòu xiànjīn fùkuǎn.
English: The supermarket only accepts cash payment.

Chinese: 我在钱包里发现了一些现金。
Pinyin: Wǒ zài qiánbāo lǐ fāxiàn le yīxiē xiànjīn.
English: I found some cash in my wallet.

Chinese: 我喜欢用现金支付，不使用信用卡。
Pinyin: Wǒ xǐhuān yòng xiànjīn zhīfù, bù shǐyòng xìnyòngkǎ.
English: I prefer paying with cash, not using a credit card.

Chinese: 他收到一大笔现金作为生日礼物。
Pinyin: Tā shōudào yī dà bǐ xiànjīn zuòwéi shēngrì lǐwù.
English: He received a large sum of cash as a birthday gift.

Chinese: 爸爸把一些现金留在钱包里备用。
Pinyin: Bàba bǎ yīxiē xiànjīn liú zài qiánbāo lǐ bèiyòng.
English: Dad keeps some cash in his wallet for emergencies.

Chinese: 这家商店不接受信用卡，只收现金。
Pinyin: Zhè jiā shāngdiàn bù jiēshòu xìnyòngkǎ, zhǐ shōu xiànjīn.
English: This shop doesn't accept credit cards, only cash.

Chinese: 我不太喜欢携带现金，因为它容易丢失。
Pinyin: Wǒ bù tài xǐhuān xiédài xiànjīn, yīnwèi tā róngyì diūshī.
English: I don't really like carrying cash because it is easy to lose.

Chinese: 旅行时最好带一些现金用于小费支付。
Pinyin: Lǚxíng shí zuìhǎo dài yīxiē xiànjīn yòngyú xiǎofèi zhīfù.
English: It's best to carry some cash for tipping when traveling.

Chinese: 现在很多人都喜欢用手机支付，而不用现金。
Pinyin: Xiànzài hěnduō rén dōu xǐhuān yòng shǒujī zhīfù, ér bùyòng xiànjīn.
English: Nowadays, many people prefer using mobile payment instead of cash.

Chinese: 我用信用卡支付账单。
Pinyin: Wǒ yòng xìnyòngkǎ zhīfù zhàngdān.
English: I pay bills with a credit card.

Chinese: 你经常使用信用卡吗？
Pinyin: Nǐ jīngcháng shǐyòng xìnyòngkǎ ma?
English: Do you often use a credit card?

Chinese: 昨天我把信用卡弄丢了。
Pinyin: Zuótiān wǒ bǎ xìnyòngkǎ nòng diū le.
English: I lost my credit card yesterday.

Chinese: 这个商店可以刷信用卡。
Pinyin: Zhège shāngdiàn kěyǐ shuā xìnyòngkǎ.
English: You can use a credit card at this store.

Chinese: 信用卡有没有限制？
Pinyin: Xìnyòngkǎ yǒu méiyǒu xiànzhì?
English: Are there any restrictions on credit cards?

Chinese: 请将信用卡的后四位号码告诉我。
Pinyin: Qǐng jiāng xìnyòngkǎ de hòu sì wèi hàomǎ gàosù wǒ.
English: Please tell me the last four digits of your credit card.

Chinese: 信用卡账单在月底寄给你。
Pinyin: Xìnyòngkǎ zhàngdān zài yuèdǐ jì gěi nǐ.
English: Your credit card bill will be sent to you at the end of the month.

Chinese: 别忘了及时还信用卡欠款。
Pinyin: Bié wàngle jíshí huán xìnyòngkǎ qiànkuǎn.
English: Don't forget to repay your credit card debt in a timely manner.

Chinese: 信用卡消费总额不能超过额度。
Pinyin: Xìnyòngkǎ xiāofèi zǒng'é bùnéng chāoguò édù.
English: The total amount of credit card spending should not exceed the limit.

Chinese: 我想申请一张信用卡。
Pinyin: Wǒ xiǎng shēnqǐng yī zhāng xìnyòngkǎ.
English: I would like to apply for a credit card.

Chinese: 我用手机扫了二维码。
Pinyin: Wǒ yòng shǒujī sǎo le èrwéimǎ.
English: I scanned the QR code with my phone.

Chinese: 请用相机扫描二维码。
Pinyin: Qǐng yòng xiàngjī sǎomiáo èrwéimǎ.
English: Please scan the QR code with a camera.

Chinese: 这个二维码可以支付。
Pinyin: Zhège èrwéimǎ kěyǐ zhīfù.
English: This QR code can be used for payment.

Chinese: 我生成了一个新的二维码。
Pinyin: Wǒ shēngchéng le yīgè xīn de èrwéimǎ.
English: I generated a new QR code.

Chinese: 请把相机对准二维码。
Pinyin: Qǐng bǎ xiàngjī duìzhǔn èrwéimǎ.
English: Please aim the camera at the QR code.

Chinese: 这个二维码有多少个字符？
Pinyin: Zhège èrwéimǎ yǒu duōshǎo gè zìfú?
English: How many characters are in this QR code?

Chinese: 请把二维码分享给其他人。
Pinyin: Qǐng bǎ èrwéimǎ fēnxiǎng gěi qítā rén.
English: Please share the QR code with others.

Chinese: 这个二维码可以用于登录。
Pinyin: Zhège èrwéimǎ kěyǐ yòngyú dēnglù.
English: This QR code can be used for login.

Chinese: 请将二维码保存到手机相册。
Pinyin: Qǐng jiāng èrwéimǎ bǎocún dào shǒujī xiàngcè.
English: Please save the QR code to the phone's photo album.

Chinese: 请用二维码扫描设备上的信息。
Pinyin: Qǐng yòng èrwéimǎ sǎomiáo shèbèi shàng de xìnxī.
English: Please use the QR code to scan the information on the device.
